And if you cannot secure it in the manner we have described, you must bind the two feet of the patient together with a strong bandage under both heels and above both knees; then let the affected leg be extended two spans more than the other; then suspend him by the head from a post, and let him hang two arm lengths off the ground; then instruct one assistant to embrace the upper thigh, and have another assistant hanging alongside the patient, who embraces it forcefully, for now the joint returns quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi; puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme; et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And when the dislocation is out of place, let the patient lie down, as we have said in the case of one who has gout, and bind one cloth tightly around the affected leg, and do the same at the foot; then place two torches, one at the head and another at the feet, then insert a torch between the patient’s thighs in the form required; and let pieces of moist cloths be placed around to prevent burns, then each attendant should extend towards him, and the physician places his hand equal to the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place him on the table and press as we have said in the case of gout, and let the patient lie on the healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And when dislocation is before us, it is necessary to quickly extend the diseased leg as I have said; and let the doctors place their efforts on being above the affected area, then press with the other hand, and stretch downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And if the dislocation is to the rear, it should not be extended downward nor lifted off the ground, but rather, he must lie as if his hip were dislocated to the rear, as we have described the position for lying on both hips; and let him be on his back, with the limb extended as previously mentioned, and one should press on the joint against a table; it will be correct when the patient extends their legs equally; then join the thighs together, apply the plaster, and bind tightly so that the hip does not move; rest for three days or four, then loosen it, and reapply the plaster; if you see them equal, tie as before, leave it for three days; then unbind it, and have him walk gently until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The knee is dislocated in three ways: namely, inward and outward, and backward; it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the signs are that you instruct the patient to bend his leg at the thigh, and if it does not bend properly, then you know it is dislocated; and the restoration of all such cases is as follows: make the patient sit upright, and extend his leg if he can, and place your back against his front, and put his foot on your feet; then take his knee in your palms, and pull between your hands, then bend both sides of the knee forcefully; and another assistant extends his foot so that the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that it bends properly at the thigh lightly; and apply a plaster, and bind the leg to the thigh firmly for three days or four, then unbind him; and do not allow the patient to walk until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not properly aligned, apply strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the thigh, until it is set right
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes bruised, and sometimes completely dislocated, both inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and it feels loose at the part where it is dislocated: the reduction is easy, and one should gently extend it with their hands when it is only bruised.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is completely dislocated, you must have the patient sit upright, and hold them firmly by the thigh with one hand above the ankle; then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, and then again with your left hand twice, then extend it upwards, and forcefully push the foot upwards; do this twice as we have said, pushing and pulling the foot; if it returns, that is good; if not, continue the work, for it will return; and if it cannot return thus, lie the patient on their back on the ground, and firmly fix a lever between their thighs, tying ropes around them to secure the patient; then hold one thigh with your hands or with a bandage, tied behind the ankle of the dislocated leg; both assistants should pull equally, and the lever should be securely placed between the patient’s thighs to keep the patient in place when extending; then place the dislocation in your hands equally, and another assistant holds the sound leg from behind, and the dislocation will quickly return.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is ready, place the plaster and wadding on, tie the foot to the leg firmly, but ensure that the bandage around the ankle behind is not too tight; then leave it for two or three days, and if the bandage loosens, retighten it; then remove it on the third day or fourth, and forbid the patient from walking for four days; and if he walks before this term, it is not certain that he will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if painful abscesses come, you must soothe them as we have said elsewhere, until they are healed.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When both are dislocated, they must be gently extended without strain, and this is an easy task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any joint of the foot's back, you must make the patient sit on a flat place or on a straight table, and put your foot under what appears to be the joints, then press hard with your foot until it rights; and when they are even, and there does not appear anything amiss, place under the sole of the foot a board two spans wide, then firmly pull it back, and leave it for three days, then release it; and let it rest until he is well.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and of dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with dislocation and one wishes to restore it, many times the patient dies: do not be presumptuous in treatment if you are not wise in the art and have not practiced long, and if you are not compassionate and slow, but not bold; and use soothing remedies for hot abscesses at the beginning, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of health; and when there is hope, now reset the limb to its place as if treating a hot abscess; and when the limb is back in place, administer soothing remedies for hot abscesses, and treat the wound properly with desiccating ointments; and if along with dislocation there is a fracture and small bones displaced, remove them and do what we have said regarding simple diseases; and beware of entering paths of fear as I have said, for it leads you according to your Creator's will, and for the wisdom of your weapon and body.
Amen	So be it
